INSERT INTO hh_household (hh_id, hh_code, hh_status_reason, hh_tel, hh_village, hhs_id, hhsr_id, swk_id, wrd_id, usr_id_create, usr_id_update, usr_date_create, usr_date_update, ofc_id)
